############################
##      Speer Events      ##
############################

add_namespace = speer

country_event = { #Speer Wins GCW
	id = speer.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.1" }
	title = speer.1.t
	desc = speer.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_speer_wins

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = speer.1.a
		add_stability = 0.3
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = WORLD.2055 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #DSR Coups Speer
	id = speer.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.2"}
	title = speer.2.t
	desc = speer.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_communists_riot

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SGR
	}

	option = { #Speer is killed
		name = speer.2.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		every_other_country = {
			limit = { has_war_with = SGR }
			set_country_flag = GCW_at_war_with_speer
		}

		GER_GCW_off_a_fucker = yes

		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { is_DSR_unit_leader = yes }
			set_nationality = DSR
		}
		DSR = {
			add_to_array = { global.GCW_contenders = THIS }

		    add_state_core = 55
		    add_state_core = 57
		    add_state_core = 56
			add_state_core = 51
			add_state_core = 775
			
			annex_country = {
				target = SGR
				transfer_troops = yes
			}

			change_tag_from = SGR

			country_event = { days = 1 id = DSR.1 }
			set_country_flag = dsr_civil_war
			inherit_technology = PREV
			load_oob = DSR

			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GCW_at_war_with_speer }
				declare_war_on = { target = DSR type = civil_war }
				clr_country_flag = GCW_at_war_with_speer
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Speer survives
		name = speer.2.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { is_DSR_unit_leader = yes }
			set_nationality = DSR
		}
		SGR = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 55 }
				DSR = { transfer_state = 55 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 56 }
				DSR = { transfer_state = 56 }
			}
			declare_war_on = { target = DSR type = civil_war }
		}
		DSR = {
			add_to_array = { global.GCW_contenders = THIS }

		    add_state_core = 55
		    add_state_core = 57
		    add_state_core = 56
			add_state_core = 51
			add_state_core = 775

			country_event = { days = 1 id = DSR.1 }
			set_country_flag = dsr_civil_war
			inherit_technology = PREV
			load_oob = DSR

			declare_war_on = { target = BGR type = civil_war }
			declare_war_on = { target = GGR type = civil_war }
			declare_war_on = { target = HGR type = civil_war }
			declare_war_on = { target = RNW type = civil_war }
			declare_war_on = { target = GER type = civil_war }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Students rise up in support of Speer
	id = speer.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.3"}
    title = speer.3.t
    desc = speer.3.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_revolt

    fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

    trigger = { tag = SGR }

    option = {
        name = speer.3.a
        add_political_power = 50
        if = {
            limit = { has_war_with = BGR }
            load_oob = SGR_students_BGR
        }
        if = {
            limit = { has_war_with = GGR }
            load_oob = SGR_students_GGR
        }
        if = {
            limit = { has_war_with = HGR }
            load_oob = SGR_students_HGR
        }
    }
}

country_event = { #Anti Heydrich Pact
	id = speer.16
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.16"}
    title = speer.16.t
    desc = speer.16.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_Army

	trigger = {
		country_exists = HGR
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = speer.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact

		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = BGR }
			BGR = { country_event = bormann.8 } #continue
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GGR }
			GGR = { country_event = goering.8 } #continue
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = speer.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BGR
				country_exists = GGR
			}
			BGR = { country_event = bormann.9 } #continue with bormann making the idea
		}
	}
}

		add_stability = -0.1
		transfer_state = 776
		transfer_state = 1026

		    country_event = {
	            id = speer.23
		        days = 31
	        }
		}
    }

	option = {
        name = speer.22.c # Siege Brandenburg and North Brandenburg

		add_political_power = -100

		transfer_state = 1025

	        }
		}
    }

		}

#Speer attempts to enter the US (FIRE FOR THE USA)
country_event = {
	id = speer.151
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.151"}
	title = speer.151.t
	desc = speer.151.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Allow him in
		name = speer.151.a
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = has_speer }
		log = "[This.GetName] accepted Speer"
		#Effects for the US here
	}
	option = { #Refuse Entry
		name = speer.151.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rejected_speer
			SWE = {
				country_event = { id = speer.152 days = 3 random = 24 }
			}
		}
		log = "[This.GetName] rejected Speer"
	}
}

#Speer attempts to enter SWEDEN (FIRE FOR SWEDEN)
country_event = {
	id = speer.152
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.152"}
	title = speer.152.t
	desc = speer.152.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yea let him in
		name = speer.152.a
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = has_speer }
		log = "[This.GetName] accepted Speer"
		#Effects for Sweden here
	}
	option = { #Nah this sux
		name = speer.152.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rejected_speer
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = social_conservative
						has_government = social_liberal
						has_government = market_liberal
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = rejected_speer }
				}
				country_event = { id = speer.153 days = 3 random = 24 }
			}
		}
		log = "[This.GetName] rejected Speer"
	}
}

#Speer attempts to enter OTHER DEMOCRATIC NATION (FIRE FOR OTHER DEMOCRATIC NATION)
country_event = {
	id = speer.153
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.153"}
	title = speer.153.t
	desc = speer.153.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yea let him in
		name = speer.153.a
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = has_speer }
		log = "[This.GetName] accepted Speer"
		#Effects for country here
	}
	option = { #Nah this sux
		name = speer.153.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rejected_speer
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = social_conservative
						has_government = social_liberal
						has_government = market_liberal
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = rejected_speer }
				}
				country_event = { id = speer.153 days = 3 random = 24 }
				ROOT = { set_temp_variable = { speer_option = 1 } }
			}
			#Speer is dead if there's nobody else to flee to
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { speer_option = 1 } } }
				set_global_flag = speer_dead
				every_country = {
					news_event = { id = speer.154 days = 3 random = 24 }
				}
				log = "[This.GetName] rejected Speer, Speer dead"
			}
		}
		log = "[This.GetName] rejected Speer"
	}
}

#Speer asks for volunteers from European nations (SCO, IRE, SWE, FIN, ROM, BUL, ITA, IBR)
country_event = {
	id = speer.160
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.160"}
	title = speer.160.t
	desc = speer.160.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		name = speer.160.a
		log = "[This.GetName] helped Speer"
		add_manpower = -2500
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_equipment
			amount = 300
			target = SGR
		}
		SGR = {
			add_manpower = 2500
			country_event = {
				id = speer.161
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 	
		name = speer.160.b
		log = "[This.GetName] didn't help Speer"
	}
}

					COG = {

							var = tempRandom
							distribution = uniform
							min = 400
							max = 1000
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {THIS.GDP = tempRandom}
						add_to_variable = {GER.money_reserves = tempRandom}
					}
				}
				30 = {
					ANG = {
						set_temp_variable = {tempRandom = 500}
						randomize_temp_variable = {
							var = tempRandom
							distribution = uniform
							min = 400
							max = 1000
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {THIS.GDP = tempRandom}
						add_to_variable = {GER.money_reserves = tempRandom}
					}
				}
				30 = {
					MZB = {
						set_temp_variable = {tempRandom = 500}
						randomize_temp_variable = {
							var = tempRandom
							distribution = uniform
							min = 400
							max = 1000
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {THIS.GDP = tempRandom}
						add_to_variable = {GER.money_reserves = tempRandom}
					}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_SAW_rob_assets_money_tt
	}

#Hidden event to fire event chains
country_event = { 
	id = speer.10004
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.10004"}
	title = speer.10004.t
	desc = speer.10004.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_speer

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#random = 24
	option = {
		name = speer.10004.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = speerflavor.90 days = 1}
					set_country_flag = SGR_danzig_slave_fired
					country_event = { id = speer.10004 days = 80 random = 60}
					modifier = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = SGR_danzig_slave_fired
							NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_phase2}
						}
						factor = 0
					}
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = tresckowgo4.6 days = 1}
					set_country_flag = SGR_tresckow_heuaktion_fired
					country_event = { id = speer.10004 days = 240 random = 60}
					modifier = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = SGR_tresckow_heuaktion_fired
							NOT = {has_country_flag = SGR_phase2}
						}
						factor = 0
					}
				}

					set_country_flag = SGR_spet_science_fired
					country_event = { id = speer.10004 days = 240 random = 60}

						OR = {

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = speer.10006.a
		DFK = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = VLG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

#Event to level down Speer's GDP growth starting in 68
country_event = { 
	id = speer.10007
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speer.10007"}

	title = speer.10007.t
	desc = speer.10007.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_speer

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = speer.10007.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {GER.GDP_growth > 0.03}
				date < 1972.1.1
				has_global_flag = german_civil_war_speervic
			}
			set_temp_variable = {tempGDP = GER.GDP_growth}
			multiply_temp_variable = {tempGDP = 0.1}
			subtract_from_variable = {GER.GDP_growth = tempGDP}
			country_event = {
				id = speer.10007
				days = 90
			}
		}
	}
}

		ai_chance = { factor = 65 }
		increase_conservative_leaning_small = yes
		decrease_regime_stab_small = yes
	}
	option = { #Prison
		name = speerpoland.20.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }
		increase_reformist_leaning_small = yes
		add_regime_stab_small = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = speerostland.6 #Speer invites Stahlecker to negotiate, speer can accept or be pressured by the party to demand more
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speerostland.6"}
	title = speerostland.6.t
	desc = speerostland.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = speerostland.6.a
		set_country_flag = ostland_negotiations_sucessful
		OST = { save_party_popularities = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = OST
				autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_reichskommissariat
			}
		}
		else = { puppet = OST }
		hidden_effect = {
			OST = { 
				apply_party_popularities = yes
				set_politics = { ruling_party = national_socialism }
			}
		}
	}	

	option = {
		name = speerostland.6.b
		country_event = { id = speerostland.7 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = speerostland.27 #Landrut transfers power to the ostland provisional government with a pat on the back
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event speerostland.27"}
	title = speerostland.27.t
	desc = speerostland.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_OST_meyer_landrut

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = speerostland.27.a
		hidden_effect = {
			OST = {
				annex_country = {
					target = MST
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				GER = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
								has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
							}
						}
						set_autonomy = {
							target = OST
							autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_reichskommissariat
						}
					}
					else = { puppet = OST }
				}
				join_zollverein = yes
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_model_colony} remove_ideas = OST_model_colony }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_model_colony2} remove_ideas = OST_model_colony2 }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_unusual_quiet} remove_ideas = OST_unusual_quiet }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_No_head} remove_ideas = OST_No_head }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_crippled_military} remove_ideas = OST_crippled_military }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_stabbed_in_the_back} remove_ideas = OST_stabbed_in_the_back }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_broken_nation} remove_ideas = OST_broken_nation }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_harsh_economic_integration} remove_ideas = OST_harsh_economic_integration }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_United_for_Ostland} remove_ideas = OST_United_for_Ostland }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_Defend_Riga_idea} remove_ideas = OST_Defend_Riga_idea }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_Prussian_Values} remove_ideas = OST_Prussian_Values }
				if = { limit = {has_idea = OST_Haste_Makes_Waste} remove_ideas = OST_Haste_Makes_Waste }
				set_cosmetic_tag = ostland_occupation_authority
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Alfred Zerbel"
					picture = "Portrait_GER_Alfred_Zerbel.dds"
					expire = "1980.1.1"
					ideology = fascism_subtype
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name =    OST_speer_occupation_government_fascism_long
					name =    OST_speer_occupation_government_fascism
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = despotism
					long_name = OST_speer_belarus_liberation_front
					name = OST_speer_belarus_liberation_front_long
				}

				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					long_name = OST_speer_united_baltic_army
					name = OST_speer_united_baltic_army_long
				}

				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					long_name = OST_speer_united_baltic_army
					name = OST_speer_united_baltic_army_long
				}

				set_party_name = {
					ideology = socialist
					long_name = OST_speer_student_movement
					name = OST_speer_student_movement_long
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 50
					national_socialism = 30
					despotism = 5
					social_conservative = 10
					socialist = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = usagertrade

country_event = { #debug
	id = usagertrade.99
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usagertrade.99"}
	title = usagertrade.99.t
	desc = usagertrade.99.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_generic_speer
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usagertrade.99.a
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = embargo
		}
		USA = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = embargo
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Military technology cooperation
	id = usagertrade.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usagertrade.1"}
	title = usagertrade.1.t
	desc = usagertrade.1.desc
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_research_lab
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usagertrade.1.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				check_variable = {national_debt < 30}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 75
				check_variable = {national_debt < 15}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				check_variable = {national_debt = 0}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { national_debt = 15 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_debt_small
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.15
			uses = 1
			category = infantry_weapons
			category = support_tech
			category = artillery
			category = armor
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = SGR_pet_relations_var
					value = 100
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_pet_trust_growth_5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				USA = {
					add_to_variable = {
						money_reserves = 15
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						bonus = 0.25
						uses = 1
						category = infantry_weapons
						category = support_tech
						category = artillery
						category = armor
					}

					tag = USA
				}
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						id = usagertrade.14
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Offer accepted
	id = usagertrade.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usagertrade.13"}
	title = usagertrade.13.t
	desc = usagertrade.13.desc
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_crate_of_guns
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usagertrade.13.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = GER_SGR_german_american_commerce_dynamic_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_SGR_german_american_commerce_dynamic_modifier }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = SGR_pet_relations_var
					value = 100
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_pet_trust_growth_10
			add_to_variable = { SGR_pet_relations_var = 10 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = SGR_pet_relations_var
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = SGR_pet_industrial_capacity
					value = 0.1
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { SGR_pet_industrial_capacity = 0.01 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_pet_industrial_capacity_tt
			clamp_variable = {
				var = SGR_pet_industrial_capacity
				min = 0
				max = 0.10
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}

					}

			}

			}
		}

					has_country_leader = {

						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = speerfrance.13
				days = 7
			}
		}
		else_if = {

				FRA = {

						ruling_only = yes
					}

				}

					country_event = {

						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		add_political_power = -20

				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = speerfrance.18
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #No

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_what_are_you_doing_tt
		hidden_effect = {

country_event = { #Erhard demands Flat Income Tax 
	id = erhardgo4.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event erhardgo4.1" }
	title = erhardgo4.1.t
	desc = erhardgo4.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_erhard
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Accept
		name = erhardgo4.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = erhardgo4.2
				days = 2
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = tno_income_taxation_elite_tax_exemptions
			add_idea = tno_income_taxation_flat_taxes
		}
	}
	option = { #Deny
		name = erhardgo4.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_SPEER_PATH
						option = GER_SPEER_PATH_REFORMER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_SPEER_PATH
						option = GER_SPEER_PATH_CONSERVATIVE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = erhardgo4.5
				days = 2
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_erhard_warning
	}
}
